These objects may be filled with solid colors, patterns, radial or linear color gradients and their borders may be stroked, both with adjustable transparency. Embedding and optional tracing of raster graphics is also supported, enabling the editor to create vector graphics from photos and other raster sources. Created shapes can be further manipulated with transformations, such as moving, rotating, scaling and skewing.\r\n\r\nhttps://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Inkscape\r\n\r\nYou can support Inkscape! https://inkscape.org/en/support-us/donate/","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9NBLGGH0BRKQ","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"Photo Editor 10","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"logo","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.3002.13510798882790695.0f14f07a-62b8-4899-b499-cd2cb30077ee.5c551304-f361-4429-9f89-cf4a56a5a08d","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"StrikethroughPrice":"8,00 kr.","DisplayPrice":"Gratis⁺","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":3.4,"RatingsCount":"20","PackageFamilyNames":["5209invention.SketchPhoto_mxj784dsfjm70"],"ContentIds":["fc52669d-ffab-4e46-db0e-d6a5fa5e0a83","9ac16fc0-e7da-f294-9b0d-0228bc814ff8","1bb5858b-ac55-310d-c3db-71ecf936502d"],"Badges":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V3.ProductBadge, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","StyleKey":"Default","Text":"SPAR 8,00 kr.","Type":"Merchandized"}],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":" ","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"Pc,Mobil","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"You Don't need to be a pro anymore to use Photo Editing software. \r\nExperience the Awesomeness in this very easy to use photo editor.
